< Text>
I order take out from here at least once a month, if not more. For whatever reason, the appetizers like the pot stickers, soup dumplings, and fried chicken are freaking good.

The entrees are less exciting, but not terrible.

My only complaint is that the pickup process is kind of screwy when it's busy. Despite having ordered ahead and seeing my food on the table, I've had to wait for 5 or 10 minutes before the 1 cashier/attendant was free to hand me my food. This is a major turn off for someone that's hungry.< /Text>
